1  Schema Globals
  Global Schema Type
    rw_ypbc_Vnfr_t_schema
  Global Schema Pointer
    rw_ypbc_Vnfr_g_schema
2  module rw-project

2.1  rw-project data
  Description
    This yang module defines project-based tenancy for RIFT.ware.
    Authorization for project access is defined in terms of RIFT.ware's
    Role-Based Access Control (RBAC) model.

2.1.1  list rw-project:project
  Description
    Configuration and state for individual projects.  RIFT.ware
    applications and projects are expected to augment this list in
    order to add configuration for projects that is specific to the
    product or application.  As such, this list contains minimal
    data defined in this yang module.

    When augmenting this element, other yang modules should prefer to
    define containers with the same name as the augmenting module.
    (Augmenting RIFT.ware modules should prefer to augment without
    the rw prefix [for new features], or should prefer to augment the
    augmented container of an existing augment, to ease future
    adoption and/or standardization.)
  Leaves
    name: name, type: STRING, description: Name of the project.
    name: description, type: STRING, description: Information about project
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-project:project/STRING
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    C,/rw-project:project
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    C,/rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    D,/rw-project:project
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    D,/rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfr.YangData.RwProject.Project
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfrYang.YangData_RwProject_Project
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    Vnfr__YangData__RwProject__Project
  C RWPB Identifiers
    Vnfr_RwProject_data_Project
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_Vnfr_RwProject_data_Project

2.1.1.1.1  list rw-project:user
  Description
    The list of Users who have been assigned Roles within this
    Project.
  Leaves
    name: user-domain, type: LEAFREF, description: The user domain.  This is the source of the user identity.
    Different domains may duplicate a user-name, but such users
    would be considered distinct by RIFT.ware.
    name: user-name, type: LEAFREF, description: The user name.  The syntax of this name depends on the domain.
    For example, if the domain is a login name, it might be limited
    to alphanumeric characters.  However, if the domain is email address,
    the syntax could include additional characters, such as the at(@) sign.
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/rw-project:project-config/rw-project:user
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/rw-project:project-config/rw-project:user[rw-project:user-name='STRING'][rw-project:user-domain='STRING']
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-project:project/STRING/project-config/user/STRING,STRING
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    C,/rw-project:project/rw-project:project-config/rw-project:user
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    C,/rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/rw-project:project-config/rw-project:user[rw-project:user-name='STRING'][rw-project:user-domain='STRING']

  Description
    The state of the Roles the User has been assigned.
  Leaves
    name: role, type: STRING, description: The Role, independent of Keys.
    name: state, type: STRING, description: The assignment of a User to a Role may be an asynchronous
    operation.  This value indicates whether the Role
    assignment is active.  If the value is 'active', then the
    assignment is complete and active.  Any other value
    indicates that Role assignment is in a transitional or
    failed state, as described in the value.
  XPath Path

2.1.1.5.1.1  list project-nsd:connection-point
  Description
    List for external connection points.
    Each NS has one or more external connection
    points. As the name implies that external
    connection points are used for connecting
    the NS to other NS or to external networks.
    Each NS exposes these connection points to
    the orchestrator. The orchestrator can
    construct network service chains by
    connecting the connection points between
    different NS.
  Leaves
    name: name, type: STRING, description: Name of the NS connection point.
    name: type, type: ENUM, description: Type of the connection point.
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/project-nsd:nsd-catalog/project-nsd:nsd/project-nsd:connection-point
  XPath Keyed Path

2.1.1.5.1.2  list project-nsd:scaling-group-descriptor
  Description
    scaling group descriptor within this network service.
    The scaling group defines a group of VNFs,
    and the ratio of VNFs in the network service
    that is used as target for scaling action
  Leaves
    name: name, type: STRING, description: Name of this scaling group.
    name: min-instance-count, type: UINT32, description: Minimum instances of the scaling group which are allowed.
    These instances are created by default when the network service
    is instantiated.
    name: max-instance-count, type: UINT32, description: Maximum instances of this scaling group that are allowed
    in a single network service. The network service scaling
    will fail, when the number of service group instances
    exceed the max-instance-count specified.
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/project-nsd:nsd-catalog/project-nsd:nsd/project-nsd:scaling-group-descriptor
  XPath Keyed Path

2.1.1.5.1.2.1  list project-nsd:scaling-policy
  Leaves
    name: name, type: STRING, description: Name of the scaling policy
    name: scaling-type, type: ENUM, description: Type of scaling
    name: enabled, type: BOOLEAN, description: Specifies if the scaling policy can be applied
    name: scale-in-operation-type, type: ENUM, description: Operation to be applied to check between scaling criterias to
    check if the scale in threshold condition has been met.
    Defaults to AND
    name: scale-out-operation-type, type: ENUM, description: Operation to be applied to check between scaling criterias to
    check if the scale out threshold condition has been met.
    Defauls to OR
    name: threshold-time, type: UINT32, description: The duration for which the criteria must hold true
    name: cooldown-time, type: UINT32, description: The duration after a scaling-in/scaling-out action has been
    triggered, for which there will be no further optional

2.1.1.5.1.13  list project-nsd:placement-groups
  Description
    List of placement groups at NS level
  Leaves
    name: name, type: STRING, description: Place group construct to define the compute resource placement strategy
    in cloud environment
    name: requirement, type: STRING, description: This is free text space used to describe the intent/rationale
    behind this placement group. This is for human consumption only
    name: strategy, type: ENUM, description: Strategy associated with this placement group
    Following values are possible
      - COLOCATION: Colocation strategy imply intent to share the physical
                    infrastructure (hypervisor/network) among all members
                    of this group.
      - ISOLATION: Isolation strategy imply intent to not share the physical
                   infrastructure (hypervisor/network) among the members
                   of this group.

2.1.1.6.1.5  list project-vnfd:connection-point
  Description
    List for external connection points. Each VNF has one
    or more external connection points that connect the VNF
    to other VNFs or to external networks. Each VNF exposes
    connection points to the orchestrator, which can construct
    network services by connecting the connection points
    between different VNFs. The NFVO will use VLDs and VNFFGs
    at the network service level to construct network services.
  Leaves
    name: name, type: STRING, description: Name of the connection point
    name: id, type: STRING, description: Identifier for the internal connection points
    name: short-name, type: STRING, description: Short name to appear as label in the UI
    name: type, type: ENUM, description: Type of the connection point.
    name: port-security-enabled, type: BOOLEAN, description: Enables the port security for the port

  Leaves

    pass as metadata during the VM creation.
    name: image, type: STRING, description: Image name for the software image.
    If the image name is found within the VNF package it will
    be uploaded to all VIM accounts during onboarding process.
    Otherwise, the image must be added to the VIM account with
    the same name as entered here.

    name: image-checksum, type: STRING, description: Image md5sum for the software image.
    The md5sum, if provided, along with the image name uniquely
    identifies an image uploaded to the CAL.

    name: cloud-init-file, type: STRING, description: Name of file with contents of cloud-init script in cloud-config format

2.1.1.6.1.7.2  container project-vnfd:guest-epa
  Leaves
    name: trusted-execution, type: BOOLEAN, description: This VM should be allocated from trusted pool
    name: mempage-size, type: ENUM, description: Memory page allocation size. If a VM requires
    hugepages, it should choose LARGE or SIZE_2MB
    or SIZE_1GB. If the VM prefers hugepages it
    should choose PREFER_LARGE.
    LARGE        : Require hugepages (either 2MB or 1GB)
    SMALL        : Doesn't require hugepages
    SIZE_2MB     : Requires 2MB hugepages
    SIZE_1GB     : Requires 1GB hugepages
    PREFER_LARGE : Application prefers hugepages
    name: cpu-pinning-policy, type: ENUM, description: CPU pinning policy describes association
    between virtual CPUs in guest and the
    physical CPUs in the host.
    DEDICATED : Virtual CPUs are pinned to
      physical CPUs
    SHARED    : Multiple VMs may share the
      same physical CPUs.
    ANY       : Any policy is acceptable for the VM
    name: cpu-thread-pinning-policy, type: ENUM, description: CPU thread pinning policy describes how to
    place the guest CPUs when the host supports
    hyper threads:
    AVOID   : Avoids placing a guest on a host
    with threads.
    SEPARATE: Places vCPUs on separate cores,
    and avoids placing two vCPUs on
    two threads of same core.
    ISOLATE : Places each vCPU on a different core,
    and places no vCPUs from a different
    guest on the same core.
    PREFER  : Attempts to place vCPUs on threads
    of the same core.
    name: numa-unaware, type: EMPTY
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/project-vnfd:vnfd-catalog/project-vnfd:vnfd/project-vnfd:vdu/project-vnfd:guest-epa

2.1.1.6.1.7.2.2  container project-vnfd:numa-node-policy
  Description
    This policy defines NUMA topology of the
    guest. Specifically identifies if the guest
    should be run on a host with one NUMA
    node or multiple NUMA nodes. As an example
    a guest might need 8 VCPUs and 4 GB of
    memory. However, it might need the VCPUs
    and memory distributed across multiple
    NUMA nodes. In this scenario, NUMA node
    1 could run with 6 VCPUs and 3GB, and
    NUMA node 2 could run with 2 VCPUs and
    1GB.
  Leaves
    name: node-cnt, type: UINT16, description: The number of NUMA nodes to expose to the VM.
    name: mem-policy, type: ENUM, description: This policy specifies how the memory should
    be allocated in a multi-node scenario.
    STRICT    : The memory must be allocated
    strictly from the memory attached
    to the NUMA node.
    PREFERRED : The memory should be allocated
    preferentially from the memory
    attached to the NUMA node
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/project-vnfd:vnfd-catalog/project-vnfd:vnfd/project-vnfd:vdu/project-vnfd:guest-epa/project-vnfd:numa-node-policy
  XPath Keyed Path

  Description
    List for internal connection points. Each VNFC

    has only one VNFC, it may not have any internal
    connection points.

2.1.1.6.1.7.8.1  container project-vnfd:virtual-interface
  Description
    Container for the virtual interface properties
  Leaves
    name: type, type: ENUM, description: Specifies the type of virtual interface
    between VM and host.
    VIRTIO          : Use the traditional VIRTIO interface.
    PCI-PASSTHROUGH : Use PCI-PASSTHROUGH interface.
    SR-IOV          : Use SR-IOV interface.
    SRIOV-DIRECT-PHYSICAL: Use SR-IOV interface with direct-physical.
    E1000           : Emulate E1000 interface.
    RTL8139         : Emulate RTL8139 interface.
    PCNET           : Emulate PCNET interface.
    OM-MGMT         : Used to specify openmano mgmt external-connection type
    AVP             : Windriver Titanium based AVP
    name: vpci, type: STRING, description: Specifies the virtual PCI address. Expressed in
    the following format dddd:dd:dd.d. For example
    0000:00:12.0. This information can be used to
    pass as metadata during the VM creation.
    name: bandwidth, type: UINT64, description: Aggregate bandwidth of the NIC.
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/project-vnfd:vnfd-catalog/project-vnfd:vnfd/project-vnfd:vdu/project-vnfd:interface/project-vnfd:virtual-interface

2.1.1.6.1.7.9  list project-vnfd:volumes
  Leaves
    name: name, type: STRING, description: Name for the volume configuration
    name: device-name, type: STRING, description: Device-name of the disk eg. vda, vdb etc
    name: resource-name, type: STRING, description: Volume name in VIM
    name: description, type: STRING, description: Description for Volume
    name: size, type: UINT64, description: Size of disk in GiB
    name: ephemeral, type: EMPTY
    name: image, type: STRING, description: Image name for the software image.
    If the image name is found within the VNF package it will
    be uploaded to all VIM accounts during onboarding process.
    Otherwise, the image must be added to the VIM account with
    the same name as entered here.

    name: image-checksum, type: STRING, description: Image md5sum for the software image.
    The md5sum, if provided, along with the image name uniquely
    identifies an image uploaded to the CAL.

    name: device-bus, type: ENUM, description: Type of disk-bus on which this disk is exposed to guest
    name: device-type, type: ENUM, description: The type of device as exposed to guest
    name: volume-type, type: STRING, description: Type of the volume

2.1.1.6.1.11  list project-vnfd:placement-groups
  Description
    List of placement groups at VNF level
  Leaves
    name: name, type: STRING, description: Place group construct to define the compute resource placement strategy
    in cloud environment
    name: requirement, type: STRING, description: This is free text space used to describe the intent/rationale
    behind this placement group. This is for human consumption only
    name: strategy, type: ENUM, description: Strategy associated with this placement group
    Following values are possible
      - COLOCATION: Colocation strategy imply intent to share the physical
                    infrastructure (hypervisor/network) among all members
                    of this group.
      - ISOLATION: Isolation strategy imply intent to not share the physical
                   infrastructure (hypervisor/network) among the members
                   of this group.
  XPath Path

2.1.1.7.1  list vnfr:vnfr
  Description
    Virtual Network Function Record (VNFR).
  Leaves
    name: id, type: STRING, description: Identifier for the VNFR.
    name: nsr-id-ref, type: STRING, description: NS instance identifier.
    This is a leafref /nsr:ns-instance-config/nsr:nsr/nsr:id
    name: member-vnf-index-ref, type: LEAFREF, description: Reference to member VNF index in Network service.
    name: remote-instance-id, type: STRING, description: Identifier VNFR instance for external RO
    name: dashboard-url, type: STRING, description: Dashboard URL
    name: name, type: STRING, description: VNFR name.
    name: short-name, type: STRING, description: VNFR short name.
    name: vendor, type: STRING, description: Vendor of the VNFR.
    name: description, type: STRING, description: Description of the VNFR.
    name: version, type: STRING, description: Version of the VNFR
    name: create-time, type: UINT32, description: Creation timestamp of this Virtual Network
    Function.  The timestamp is expressed as
    seconds since unix epoch - 1970-01-01T00:00:00Z
    name: vnfd-ref, type: LEAFREF, description: Reference to VNFD
    name: operational-status, type: ENUM, description: The operational status of the VNFR instance
    pre-init            : The VNF before Input Param Substitution.
    init                : The VNF has just started.
    vl-init-phase       : The internal VLs in the VNF are being instantiated.
    secgrp-init-phase   : The security groups in the VNF are being instantiated.
    vm-init-phase       : The VMs for VDUs in the VNF are being instantiated.
    running             : The VNF is in running state.
    terminate           : The VNF is being terminated.
    vm-terminate-phase  : The VMs in the VNF are being terminated.
    secgrp-terminate-phase   : The security groups in the VNF are being terminated
    vl-terminate-phase  : The internal VLs in the VNF are being terminated.
    terminated          : The VNF is in the terminated state.
    failed              : The VNF instantiation failed

    name: config-status, type: ENUM, description: The configuration status of the NS instance
    configuring: At least one of the VNFs in this instance is in configuring state
    configured:  All the VNFs in this NS instance are configured or config-not-needed state
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr[vnfr:id='STRING']

2.1.1.7.1.1.5  list vnfr:connection-point
  Description
    List for external connection points. Each VNF has one
    or more external connection points that connect the VNF
    to other VNFs or to external networks. Each VNF exposes
    connection points to the orchestrator, which can construct
    network services by connecting the connection points
    between different VNFs. The NFVO will use VLDs and VNFFGs
    at the network service level to construct network services.
  Leaves
    name: name, type: STRING, description: Name of the connection point
    name: id, type: STRING, description: Identifier for the internal connection points
    name: short-name, type: STRING, description: Short name to appear as label in the UI
    name: type, type: ENUM, description: Type of the connection point.
    name: port-security-enabled, type: BOOLEAN, description: Enables the port security for the port

  Leaves

    the following format dddd:dd:dd.d. For example
    0000:00:12.0. This information can be used to
    pass as metadata during the VM creation.
    name: image, type: STRING, description: Image name for the software image.
    If the image name is found within the VNF package it will
    be uploaded to all VIM accounts during onboarding process.
    Otherwise, the image must be added to the VIM account with
    the same name as entered here.

    name: image-checksum, type: STRING, description: Image md5sum for the software image.
    The md5sum, if provided, along with the image name uniquely
    identifies an image uploaded to the CAL.

    name: cloud-init, type: STRING, description: Contents of cloud-init script, provided inline, in cloud-config format
    name: cloud-init-file, type: STRING, description: Name of file with contents of cloud-init script in cloud-config format

2.1.1.7.1.1.7.2  container vnfr:guest-epa
  Leaves
    name: trusted-execution, type: BOOLEAN, description: This VM should be allocated from trusted pool
    name: mempage-size, type: ENUM, description: Memory page allocation size. If a VM requires
    hugepages, it should choose LARGE or SIZE_2MB
    or SIZE_1GB. If the VM prefers hugepages it
    should choose PREFER_LARGE.
    LARGE        : Require hugepages (either 2MB or 1GB)
    SMALL        : Doesn't require hugepages
    SIZE_2MB     : Requires 2MB hugepages
    SIZE_1GB     : Requires 1GB hugepages
    PREFER_LARGE : Application prefers hugepages
    name: cpu-pinning-policy, type: ENUM, description: CPU pinning policy describes association
    between virtual CPUs in guest and the
    physical CPUs in the host.
    DEDICATED : Virtual CPUs are pinned to
      physical CPUs
    SHARED    : Multiple VMs may share the
      same physical CPUs.
    ANY       : Any policy is acceptable for the VM
    name: cpu-thread-pinning-policy, type: ENUM, description: CPU thread pinning policy describes how to
    place the guest CPUs when the host supports
    hyper threads:
    AVOID   : Avoids placing a guest on a host
    with threads.
    SEPARATE: Places vCPUs on separate cores,
    and avoids placing two vCPUs on
    two threads of same core.
    ISOLATE : Places each vCPU on a different core,
    and places no vCPUs from a different
    guest on the same core.
    PREFER  : Attempts to place vCPUs on threads
    of the same core.
    name: numa-unaware, type: EMPTY
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr/vnfr:vnfd/vnfr:vdu/vnfr:guest-epa
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:vnfd/vnfr:vdu[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:guest-epa
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-project:project/STRING/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr/STRING/vnfd/vdu/STRING/guest-epa

2.1.1.7.1.1.7.2.2  container vnfr:numa-node-policy
  Description
    This policy defines NUMA topology of the
    guest. Specifically identifies if the guest
    should be run on a host with one NUMA
    node or multiple NUMA nodes. As an example
    a guest might need 8 VCPUs and 4 GB of
    memory. However, it might need the VCPUs
    and memory distributed across multiple
    NUMA nodes. In this scenario, NUMA node
    1 could run with 6 VCPUs and 3GB, and
    NUMA node 2 could run with 2 VCPUs and
    1GB.
  Leaves
    name: node-cnt, type: UINT16, description: The number of NUMA nodes to expose to the VM.
    name: mem-policy, type: ENUM, description: This policy specifies how the memory should
    be allocated in a multi-node scenario.
    STRICT    : The memory must be allocated
    strictly from the memory attached
    to the NUMA node.
    PREFERRED : The memory should be allocated
    preferentially from the memory
    attached to the NUMA node
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr/vnfr:vnfd/vnfr:vdu/vnfr:guest-epa/vnfr:numa-node-policy
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:vnfd/vnfr:vdu[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:guest-epa/vnfr:numa-node-policy
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-project:project/STRING/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr/STRING/vnfd/vdu/STRING/guest-epa/numa-node-policy
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    D,/rw-project:project/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr/vnfr:vnfd/vnfr:vdu/vnfr:guest-epa/vnfr:numa-node-policy
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    D,/rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:vnfd/vnfr:vdu[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:guest-epa/vnfr:numa-node-policy

2.1.1.7.1.1.7.8.1  container vnfr:virtual-interface
  Description
    Container for the virtual interface properties
  Leaves
    name: type, type: ENUM, description: Specifies the type of virtual interface
    between VM and host.
    VIRTIO          : Use the traditional VIRTIO interface.
    PCI-PASSTHROUGH : Use PCI-PASSTHROUGH interface.
    SR-IOV          : Use SR-IOV interface.
    SRIOV-DIRECT-PHYSICAL: Use SR-IOV interface with direct-physical.
    E1000           : Emulate E1000 interface.
    RTL8139         : Emulate RTL8139 interface.
    PCNET           : Emulate PCNET interface.
    OM-MGMT         : Used to specify openmano mgmt external-connection type
    AVP             : Windriver Titanium based AVP
    name: vpci, type: STRING, description: Specifies the virtual PCI address. Expressed in
    the following format dddd:dd:dd.d. For example
    0000:00:12.0. This information can be used to
    pass as metadata during the VM creation.
    name: bandwidth, type: UINT64, description: Aggregate bandwidth of the NIC.
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr/vnfr:vnfd/vnfr:vdu/vnfr:interface/vnfr:virtual-interface
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:vnfd/vnfr:vdu[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:interface[vnfr:name='STRING']/vnfr:virtual-interface

2.1.1.7.1.1.11  list vnfr:placement-groups
  Description
    List of placement groups at VNF level
  Leaves
    name: name, type: STRING, description: Place group construct to define the compute resource placement strategy
    in cloud environment
    name: requirement, type: STRING, description: This is free text space used to describe the intent/rationale
    behind this placement group. This is for human consumption only
    name: strategy, type: ENUM, description: Strategy associated with this placement group
    Following values are possible
      - COLOCATION: Colocation strategy imply intent to share the physical
                    infrastructure (hypervisor/network) among all members
                    of this group.
      - ISOLATION: Isolation strategy imply intent to not share the physical
                   infrastructure (hypervisor/network) among the members
                   of this group.
  XPath Path

2.1.1.7.1.5  list vnfr:connection-point
  Description
    List for external connection points. Each VNF has one
    or more external connection points. As the name
    implies that external connection points are used for
    connecting the VNF to other VNFs or to external networks.
    Each VNF exposes these connection points to the
    orchestrator. The orchestrator can construct network
    services by connecting the connection points between
    different VNFs. The NFVO will use VLDs and VNFFGs at
    the network service level to construct network services.
  Leaves
    name: name, type: STRING, description: Name of the connection point
    name: id, type: STRING, description: Identifier for the internal connection points
    name: short-name, type: STRING, description: Short name to appear as label in the UI
    name: type, type: ENUM, description: Type of the connection point.
    name: port-security-enabled, type: BOOLEAN, description: Enables the port security for the port
    name: vlr-ref, type: LEAFREF, description: Reference to the VLR id associated with this connection point
    name: mac-address, type: STRING, description: MAC address assigned to the external connection point
    name: connection-point-id, type: STRING, description: This is VIM assigned identifier for thsi connection point
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr/vnfr:connection-point
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:connection-point[vnfr:name='STRING']
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-project:project/STRING/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr/STRING/connection-point/STRING
  RW Keyspec XPath Path

  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    D,/rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:connection-point[vnfr:name='STRING']

  Description

  Leaves
    name: id, type: STRING, description: Unique id for the VDU

    name: vm-management-ip, type: UNION, description: VM Private Management IP address
    name: preexisting-resource-name, type: STRING, description: Name of the preexisting virtual machine in the VIM
    name: delete-on-terminate, type: BOOLEAN, description: Controls the deletion of preexisting virtual machine in VIM
    name: console-url, type: STRING, description: Console URL for this VDU, if available
    name: operational-status, type: ENUM, description: The operational status of the VDU
    init                : The VDU has just started.
    vm-init-phase       : The VDUs in the VNF is being created in VIM.
    vm-alloc-pending    : The  VM alloc is pending in VIM
    running             : The VDU is active in VM
    terminate           : The VDU is being terminated
    vm-terminate-phase  : The VDU in the VNF is being terminated in VIM.
    terminated          : The VDU is in the terminated state.
    failed              : The VDU  instantiation failed.

2.1.1.7.1.7.2  container vnfr:guest-epa
  Leaves
    name: trusted-execution, type: BOOLEAN, description: This VM should be allocated from trusted pool
    name: mempage-size, type: ENUM, description: Memory page allocation size. If a VM requires
    hugepages, it should choose LARGE or SIZE_2MB
    or SIZE_1GB. If the VM prefers hugepages it
    should choose PREFER_LARGE.
    LARGE        : Require hugepages (either 2MB or 1GB)
    SMALL        : Doesn't require hugepages
    SIZE_2MB     : Requires 2MB hugepages
    SIZE_1GB     : Requires 1GB hugepages
    PREFER_LARGE : Application prefers hugepages
    name: cpu-pinning-policy, type: ENUM, description: CPU pinning policy describes association
    between virtual CPUs in guest and the
    physical CPUs in the host.
    DEDICATED : Virtual CPUs are pinned to
      physical CPUs
    SHARED    : Multiple VMs may share the
      same physical CPUs.
    ANY       : Any policy is acceptable for the VM
    name: cpu-thread-pinning-policy, type: ENUM, description: CPU thread pinning policy describes how to
    place the guest CPUs when the host supports
    hyper threads:
    AVOID   : Avoids placing a guest on a host
    with threads.
    SEPARATE: Places vCPUs on separate cores,
    and avoids placing two vCPUs on
    two threads of same core.
    ISOLATE : Places each vCPU on a different core,
    and places no vCPUs from a different
    guest on the same core.
    PREFER  : Attempts to place vCPUs on threads
    of the same core.
    name: numa-unaware, type: EMPTY
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr/vnfr:vdur/vnfr:guest-epa
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:vdur[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:guest-epa
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-project:project/STRING/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr/STRING/vdur/STRING/guest-epa
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    D,/rw-project:project/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr/vnfr:vdur/vnfr:guest-epa
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    D,/rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:vdur[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:guest-epa
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfr.YangData.RwProject.Project.VnfrCatalog.Vnfr.Vdur.GuestEpa

2.1.1.7.1.7.2.2  container vnfr:numa-node-policy
  Description
    This policy defines NUMA topology of the
    guest. Specifically identifies if the guest
    should be run on a host with one NUMA
    node or multiple NUMA nodes. As an example
    a guest might need 8 VCPUs and 4 GB of
    memory. However, it might need the VCPUs
    and memory distributed across multiple
    NUMA nodes. In this scenario, NUMA node
    1 could run with 6 VCPUs and 3GB, and
    NUMA node 2 could run with 2 VCPUs and
    1GB.
  Leaves
    name: node-cnt, type: UINT16, description: The number of NUMA nodes to expose to the VM.
    name: mem-policy, type: ENUM, description: This policy specifies how the memory should
    be allocated in a multi-node scenario.
    STRICT    : The memory must be allocated
    strictly from the memory attached
    to the NUMA node.
    PREFERRED : The memory should be allocated
    preferentially from the memory
    attached to the NUMA node
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr/vnfr:vdur/vnfr:guest-epa/vnfr:numa-node-policy
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:vdur[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:guest-epa/vnfr:numa-node-policy
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-project:project/STRING/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr/STRING/vdur/STRING/guest-epa/numa-node-policy
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    D,/rw-project:project/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr/vnfr:vdur/vnfr:guest-epa/vnfr:numa-node-policy
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    D,/rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/vnfr:vnfr-catalog/vnfr:vnfr[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:vdur[vnfr:id='STRING']/vnfr:guest-epa/vnfr:numa-node-policy
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfr.YangData.RwProject.Project.VnfrCatalog.Vnfr.Vdur.GuestEpa.NumaNodePolicy

2.1.1.7.1.7.8  list vnfr:internal-connection-point
  Description
    List for internal connection points. Each VNFC
    has zero or more internal connection points.
    Internal connection points are used for connecting
    the VNF components internal to the VNF. If a VNF
    has only one VNFC, it may not have any internal
    connection points.
  Leaves
    name: name, type: STRING, description: Name of the connection point
    name: id, type: STRING, description: Identifier for the internal connection points
    name: short-name, type: STRING, description: Short name to appear as label in the UI
    name: type, type: ENUM, description: Type of the connection point.
    name: port-security-enabled, type: BOOLEAN, description: Enables the port security for the port
    name: mac-address, type: STRING, description: MAC address assigned to the internal connection point

2.1.1.7.1.7.9.1  container vnfr:virtual-interface
  Description
    Container for the virtual interface properties
  Leaves
    name: type, type: ENUM, description: Specifies the type of virtual interface
    between VM and host.
    VIRTIO          : Use the traditional VIRTIO interface.
    PCI-PASSTHROUGH : Use PCI-PASSTHROUGH interface.
    SR-IOV          : Use SR-IOV interface.
    name: bandwidth, type: UINT64, description: Aggregate bandwidth of the NIC.
    name: ovs-offload, type: ENUM, description: Defines if the NIC supports OVS offload.
    MANDATORY : OVS offload support in the NIC is mandatory.
    PREFERRED : OVS offload support in the NIC is preferred.
    name: vendor-id, type: STRING, description: Specifies the vendor specific id for
    the device. This is used when a NIC from
    specific HW vendor is required.
    name: datapath-library, type: STRING, description: Specifies the name and version of the datapath
    library the NIC is expected to support.
    name: provider-network-name, type: STRING, description: Name of the provider network to which this
    NIC is attached.
  XPath Path

2.1.1.7.1.7.10  list vnfr:placement-groups-info
  Description

      Placement groups to which this VDU belongs and its
      cloud construct
  Leaves
    name: name, type: STRING, description: Place group construct to define the compute resource placement strategy
    in cloud environment
    name: requirement, type: STRING, description: This is free text space used to describe the intent/rationale
    behind this placement group. This is for human consumption only
    name: strategy, type: ENUM, description: Strategy associated with this placement group
    Following values are possible
      - COLOCATION: Colocation strategy imply intent to share the physical
                    infrastructure (hypervisor/network) among all members
                    of this group.
      - ISOLATION: Isolation strategy imply intent to not share the physical
                   infrastructure (hypervisor/network) among the members
                   of this group.

    name: cloud-type, type: ENUM
    name: aws-construct, type: EMPTY
    name: mock-construct, type: EMPTY
    name: cloudsim-construct, type: EMPTY
  XPath Path

2.1.1.7.1.10  list vnfr:placement-groups-info
  Description

      Placement groups to which this VDU belongs and its
      cloud construct
  Leaves
    name: name, type: STRING, description: Place group construct to define the compute resource placement strategy
    in cloud environment
    name: requirement, type: STRING, description: This is free text space used to describe the intent/rationale
    behind this placement group. This is for human consumption only
    name: strategy, type: ENUM, description: Strategy associated with this placement group
    Following values are possible
      - COLOCATION: Colocation strategy imply intent to share the physical
                    infrastructure (hypervisor/network) among all members
                    of this group.
      - ISOLATION: Isolation strategy imply intent to not share the physical
                   infrastructure (hypervisor/network) among the members
                   of this group.

    name: cloud-type, type: ENUM
    name: aws-construct, type: EMPTY
    name: mock-construct, type: EMPTY
    name: cloudsim-construct, type: EMPTY

2.1.1.10.9.2  container rwcal:guest-epa
  Leaves
    name: trusted-execution, type: BOOLEAN, description: This VM should be allocated from trusted pool
    name: mempage-size, type: ENUM, description: Memory page allocation size. If a VM requires
    hugepages, it should choose LARGE or SIZE_2MB
    or SIZE_1GB. If the VM prefers hugepages it
    should choose PREFER_LARGE.
    LARGE        : Require hugepages (either 2MB or 1GB)
    SMALL        : Doesn't require hugepages
    SIZE_2MB     : Requires 2MB hugepages
    SIZE_1GB     : Requires 1GB hugepages
    PREFER_LARGE : Application prefers hugepages
    name: cpu-pinning-policy, type: ENUM, description: CPU pinning policy describes association
    between virtual CPUs in guest and the
    physical CPUs in the host.
    DEDICATED : Virtual CPUs are pinned to
      physical CPUs
    SHARED    : Multiple VMs may share the
      same physical CPUs.
    ANY       : Any policy is acceptable for the VM
    name: cpu-thread-pinning-policy, type: ENUM, description: CPU thread pinning policy describes how to
    place the guest CPUs when the host supports
    hyper threads:
    AVOID   : Avoids placing a guest on a host
    with threads.
    SEPARATE: Places vCPUs on separate cores,
    and avoids placing two vCPUs on
    two threads of same core.
    ISOLATE : Places each vCPU on a different core,
    and places no vCPUs from a different
    guest on the same core.
    PREFER  : Attempts to place vCPUs on threads
    of the same core.
    name: numa-unaware, type: EMPTY
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/rwcal:vim-resources/rwcal:flavorinfo-list/rwcal:guest-epa
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/rwcal:vim-resources/rwcal:flavorinfo-list[rwcal:id='STRING']/rwcal:guest-epa
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-project:project/STRING/rwcal:vim-resources/flavorinfo-list/STRING/guest-epa
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    D,/rw-project:project/rwcal:vim-resources/rwcal:flavorinfo-list/rwcal:guest-epa

2.1.1.10.9.2.2  container rwcal:numa-node-policy
  Description
    This policy defines NUMA topology of the
    guest. Specifically identifies if the guest
    should be run on a host with one NUMA
    node or multiple NUMA nodes. As an example
    a guest might need 8 VCPUs and 4 GB of
    memory. However, it might need the VCPUs
    and memory distributed across multiple
    NUMA nodes. In this scenario, NUMA node
    1 could run with 6 VCPUs and 3GB, and
    NUMA node 2 could run with 2 VCPUs and
    1GB.
  Leaves
    name: node-cnt, type: UINT16, description: The number of NUMA nodes to expose to the VM.
    name: mem-policy, type: ENUM, description: This policy specifies how the memory should
    be allocated in a multi-node scenario.
    STRICT    : The memory must be allocated
    strictly from the memory attached
    to the NUMA node.
    PREFERRED : The memory should be allocated
    preferentially from the memory
    attached to the NUMA node
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/rwcal:vim-resources/rwcal:flavorinfo-list/rwcal:guest-epa/rwcal:numa-node-policy
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/rwcal:vim-resources/rwcal:flavorinfo-list[rwcal:id='STRING']/rwcal:guest-epa/rwcal:numa-node-policy
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-project:project/STRING/rwcal:vim-resources/flavorinfo-list/STRING/guest-epa/numa-node-policy
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    D,/rw-project:project/rwcal:vim-resources/rwcal:flavorinfo-list/rwcal:guest-epa/rwcal:numa-node-policy
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    D,/rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/rwcal:vim-resources/rwcal:flavorinfo-list[rwcal:id='STRING']/rwcal:guest-epa/rwcal:numa-node-policy

2.1.1.20.2  container rwcal:guest-epa
  Leaves
    name: trusted-execution, type: BOOLEAN, description: This VM should be allocated from trusted pool
    name: mempage-size, type: ENUM, description: Memory page allocation size. If a VM requires
    hugepages, it should choose LARGE or SIZE_2MB
    or SIZE_1GB. If the VM prefers hugepages it
    should choose PREFER_LARGE.
    LARGE        : Require hugepages (either 2MB or 1GB)
    SMALL        : Doesn't require hugepages
    SIZE_2MB     : Requires 2MB hugepages
    SIZE_1GB     : Requires 1GB hugepages
    PREFER_LARGE : Application prefers hugepages
    name: cpu-pinning-policy, type: ENUM, description: CPU pinning policy describes association
    between virtual CPUs in guest and the
    physical CPUs in the host.
    DEDICATED : Virtual CPUs are pinned to
      physical CPUs
    SHARED    : Multiple VMs may share the
      same physical CPUs.
    ANY       : Any policy is acceptable for the VM
    name: cpu-thread-pinning-policy, type: ENUM, description: CPU thread pinning policy describes how to
    place the guest CPUs when the host supports
    hyper threads:
    AVOID   : Avoids placing a guest on a host
    with threads.
    SEPARATE: Places vCPUs on separate cores,
    and avoids placing two vCPUs on
    two threads of same core.
    ISOLATE : Places each vCPU on a different core,
    and places no vCPUs from a different
    guest on the same core.
    PREFER  : Attempts to place vCPUs on threads
    of the same core.
    name: numa-unaware, type: EMPTY
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/rwcal:vdu-init-params/rwcal:guest-epa
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/rwcal:vdu-init-params/rwcal:guest-epa
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-project:project/STRING/rwcal:vdu-init-params/guest-epa
  RW Keyspec XPath Path

2.1.1.20.2.2  container rwcal:numa-node-policy
  Description
    This policy defines NUMA topology of the
    guest. Specifically identifies if the guest
    should be run on a host with one NUMA
    node or multiple NUMA nodes. As an example
    a guest might need 8 VCPUs and 4 GB of
    memory. However, it might need the VCPUs
    and memory distributed across multiple
    NUMA nodes. In this scenario, NUMA node
    1 could run with 6 VCPUs and 3GB, and
    NUMA node 2 could run with 2 VCPUs and
    1GB.
  Leaves
    name: node-cnt, type: UINT16, description: The number of NUMA nodes to expose to the VM.
    name: mem-policy, type: ENUM, description: This policy specifies how the memory should
    be allocated in a multi-node scenario.
    STRICT    : The memory must be allocated
    strictly from the memory attached
    to the NUMA node.
    PREFERRED : The memory should be allocated
    preferentially from the memory
    attached to the NUMA node
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/rwcal:vdu-init-params/rwcal:guest-epa/rwcal:numa-node-policy
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/rwcal:vdu-init-params/rwcal:guest-epa/rwcal:numa-node-policy
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-project:project/STRING/rwcal:vdu-init-params/guest-epa/numa-node-policy
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    C,/rw-project:project/rwcal:vdu-init-params/rwcal:guest-epa/rwcal:numa-node-policy
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    C,/rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/rwcal:vdu-init-params/rwcal:guest-epa/rwcal:numa-node-policy
  Protobuf Type
    .rwcal.YangData.RwProject.Project.VduInitParams.GuestEpa.NumaNodePolicy
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwcalYang.YangData_RwProject_Project_VduInitParams_GuestEpa_NumaNodePolicy
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    Rwcal__YangData__RwProject__Project__VduInitParams__GuestEpa__NumaNodePolicy
  C RWPB Identifiers

  Leaves

    name: vpci, type: STRING, description: Specifies the virtual PCI address. Expressed in

    0000:00:12.0. This information can be used to
    pass as metadata during the VM creation.
    name: security-group-name, type: STRING, description: Name of the security group
    name: port-security-enabled, type: BOOLEAN, description: Enables the port security
    name: mac-address, type: STRING, description: MAC address for the port
    name: number-of-ipv4-addresses, type: UINT16, description: Number of IP addresses to be assigned.
    name: number-of-ipv6-addresses, type: UINT16, description: Number of IP addresses to be assigned.
    name: ipv4-subnet, type: STRING, description: name or id of the subnet
    name: ipv6-subnet, type: STRING, description: name or id of the subnet
    name: type, type: ENUM, description: Specifies the type of connection point
    VIRTIO          : Use the traditional VIRTIO interface.
    PCI-PASSTHROUGH : Use PCI-PASSTHROUGH interface.
    SR-IOV          : Use SR-IOV interface.
    SRIOV-DIRECT-PHYSICAL: Use SR-IOV interface with direct-physical.
    E1000           : Emulate E1000 interface.
    RTL8139         : Emulate RTL8139 interface.
    PCNET           : Emulate PCNET interface.
    AVP             : Windriver AVP
    VPORT           : Virtual Port.

2.1.1.23.1  list rwcal:volumes
  Leaves
    name: name, type: STRING, description: Name of the disk-volumes, e.g. vda, vdb etc
    name: description, type: STRING, description: Description for Volume
    name: size, type: UINT64, description: Size of disk in GiB
    name: ephemeral, type: EMPTY
    name: image, type: STRING, description: Image name for the software image.
    If the image name is found within the VNF package it will
    be uploaded to all VIM accounts during onboarding process.
    Otherwise, the image must be added to the VIM account with
    the same name as entered here.

    name: image-checksum, type: STRING, description: Image md5sum for the software image.
    The md5sum, if provided, along with the image name uniquely
    identifies an image uploaded to the CAL.

    name: device-bus, type: ENUM, description: Type of disk-bus on which this disk is exposed to guest
    name: device-type, type: ENUM, description: The type of device as exposed to guest
    name: volume-type, type: STRING, description: Type of the volume
    name: boot-volume, type: BOOLEAN, description: This flag indicates if this is boot volume or not
    name: boot-priority, type: INT32, description: Boot priority associated with volume, Zero based integer

2.1.1.25.6.2  container rwcal:guest-epa
  Leaves
    name: trusted-execution, type: BOOLEAN, description: This VM should be allocated from trusted pool
    name: mempage-size, type: ENUM, description: Memory page allocation size. If a VM requires
    hugepages, it should choose LARGE or SIZE_2MB
    or SIZE_1GB. If the VM prefers hugepages it
    should choose PREFER_LARGE.
    LARGE        : Require hugepages (either 2MB or 1GB)
    SMALL        : Doesn't require hugepages
    SIZE_2MB     : Requires 2MB hugepages
    SIZE_1GB     : Requires 1GB hugepages
    PREFER_LARGE : Application prefers hugepages
    name: cpu-pinning-policy, type: ENUM, description: CPU pinning policy describes association
    between virtual CPUs in guest and the
    physical CPUs in the host.
    DEDICATED : Virtual CPUs are pinned to
      physical CPUs
    SHARED    : Multiple VMs may share the
      same physical CPUs.
    ANY       : Any policy is acceptable for the VM
    name: cpu-thread-pinning-policy, type: ENUM, description: CPU thread pinning policy describes how to
    place the guest CPUs when the host supports
    hyper threads:
    AVOID   : Avoids placing a guest on a host
    with threads.
    SEPARATE: Places vCPUs on separate cores,
    and avoids placing two vCPUs on
    two threads of same core.
    ISOLATE : Places each vCPU on a different core,
    and places no vCPUs from a different
    guest on the same core.
    PREFER  : Attempts to place vCPUs on threads
    of the same core.
    name: numa-unaware, type: EMPTY
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/rwcal:vnf-resources/rwcal:vdu-info-list/rwcal:guest-epa
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/rwcal:vnf-resources/rwcal:vdu-info-list[rwcal:vdu-id='STRING']/rwcal:guest-epa
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-project:project/STRING/rwcal:vnf-resources/vdu-info-list/STRING/guest-epa
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    D,/rw-project:project/rwcal:vnf-resources/rwcal:vdu-info-list/rwcal:guest-epa
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    D,/rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/rwcal:vnf-resources/rwcal:vdu-info-list[rwcal:vdu-id='STRING']/rwcal:guest-epa
  Protobuf Type
    .rwcal.YangData.RwProject.Project.VnfResources.VduInfoList.GuestEpa

2.1.1.25.6.2.2  container rwcal:numa-node-policy
  Description
    This policy defines NUMA topology of the
    guest. Specifically identifies if the guest
    should be run on a host with one NUMA
    node or multiple NUMA nodes. As an example
    a guest might need 8 VCPUs and 4 GB of
    memory. However, it might need the VCPUs
    and memory distributed across multiple
    NUMA nodes. In this scenario, NUMA node
    1 could run with 6 VCPUs and 3GB, and
    NUMA node 2 could run with 2 VCPUs and
    1GB.
  Leaves
    name: node-cnt, type: UINT16, description: The number of NUMA nodes to expose to the VM.
    name: mem-policy, type: ENUM, description: This policy specifies how the memory should
    be allocated in a multi-node scenario.
    STRICT    : The memory must be allocated
    strictly from the memory attached
    to the NUMA node.
    PREFERRED : The memory should be allocated
    preferentially from the memory
    attached to the NUMA node
  XPath Path
    /rw-project:project/rwcal:vnf-resources/rwcal:vdu-info-list/rwcal:guest-epa/rwcal:numa-node-policy
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/rwcal:vnf-resources/rwcal:vdu-info-list[rwcal:vdu-id='STRING']/rwcal:guest-epa/rwcal:numa-node-policy
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-project:project/STRING/rwcal:vnf-resources/vdu-info-list/STRING/guest-epa/numa-node-policy
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    D,/rw-project:project/rwcal:vnf-resources/rwcal:vdu-info-list/rwcal:guest-epa/rwcal:numa-node-policy
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    D,/rw-project:project[rw-project:name='STRING']/rwcal:vnf-resources/rwcal:vdu-info-list[rwcal:vdu-id='STRING']/rwcal:guest-epa/rwcal:numa-node-policy

3.1.1.1  container vnfr:alarm
  Leaves
    name: alarm-id, type: STRING, description: This field is reserved for the identifier assigned by the VIM provider
    name: name, type: STRING, description: A human readable string to identify the alarm
    name: description, type: STRING, description: A description of this alarm
    name: vdur-id, type: STRING, description: The identifier of the VDUR that the alarm is associated with
    name: repeat, type: BOOLEAN, description: This flag indicates whether the alarm should be repeatedly emitted
    while the associated threshold has been crossed.
    name: enabled, type: BOOLEAN, description: This flag indicates whether the alarm has been enabled or
    disabled.
    name: severity, type: ENUM, description: A measure of the importance or urgency of the alarm
    name: metric, type: ENUM, description: The metric to be tracked by this alarm.
    name: statistic, type: ENUM, description: The type of metric statistic that is tracked by this alarm
    name: operation, type: ENUM, description: The relational operator used to define whether an alarm should be
    triggered in certain scenarios, such as if the metric statistic
    goes above or below a specified value.
    name: value, type: DECIMAL64, description: This value defines the threshold that, if crossed, will trigger
    the alarm.
    name: period, type: UINT32, description: The period defines the length of time (seconds) that the metric
    data are collected over in oreder to evaluate the chosen
    statistic.
    name: evaluations, type: UINT32, description: Defines the length of time (seconds) in which metric data are
    collected in order to evaluate the chosen statistic.
  XPath Path
    /vnfr:create-alarm/vnfr:alarm
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfr:create-alarm/vnfr:alarm
  RW.REST URI Path
    /input/alarm
